If you receive WPBN or WGTU over an antenna, you will need rescan your television channels starting on October 9, 2019. by Devon Mahieu MANISTEE COUNTY, Mich., (WPBN/WGTU) -- Multiple crews are on the scene of a fire at a recycling plant in Maple Grove Township. It happened just before 4 p.m. Tuesday at the Bay Area Recycling for Charity Building right outside the Village of Kaleva. We ' re told the facility recycles mattresses and electronics. The plant manager says four people were in the building when the fire started but got out safely. Firefighters say their goal at this point is to control the blaze. We have a crew on scene and will continue to update you as we learn more.
